I think when we closely examine the facts, we can discern that - if the two rbrs are actually equal, that the only difference, besides driver quality, is how and when they did their stints on which tires.  Checo started on Meds, Ver on Hards.  Now, this is when the car is heaviest, with a full tank.  As we saw, the Meds of Checo wore down immediately, suggesting that the extra weight was a real game changer.  The Hards, on the other hand, seemed to perform really well under load, and got progressively better in the later laps.  By the time of the switch (Checo to Meds, Ver to Med), the cars were extremly light, and the Meds were absolutely awesome under the light load, whereas the Hards did not "wear down" enough to be anywhere near competitive.  This seems to be the explanation for the ability of one car to be able to cover a 20s gap and then to pass the other.
